box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在这个建筑里，一共6个房间，象征6重梦境，左中右三条流线象征着三种在梦境中穿越的方式。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">当然，这种转译方式是在平面中进行，也就是说是<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">二维</strong>的，而我们也可以进行<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">三维</strong>转译，<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在竖向上呈现《盗梦空间》的故事情节</strong>。比方说这样：</p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">6层维度的空间变成6层平面，中间的<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">螺旋楼梯</strong>同时包含着上下两种功能，暗示着人可以自主选择进入下一层梦境或者Kick回上一层梦境。</p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n    <section style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">什么是叙事化建筑？</strong></p> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n  </section> \n </section> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">自上世纪六七十年代以后，对于<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">现代主义机械理性</strong>的批判不绝于耳。为了追求突破，建筑学从跨学科的角度不断寻求新的研究范式，重新思考建筑的创作活动。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497030768052.jpg\" title=\"1602497030768052.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012115632_调整大小.jpg\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这样打破次元壁的结果使得建筑思潮在当时百花齐放，建筑学一度变成了<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">建筑XX学</strong>。比如<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">建筑类型学，建筑现象学，建筑心理学</strong>等等。而建筑与文学的碰撞，则带来了<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">建筑叙事学</strong>。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">20世纪80年代初，时任AA教授的<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">伯纳德·屈米</strong><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(160, 160, 160);\">（Bernard Tschumi）</span>与<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">尼格尔·库特斯</strong><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(160, 160, 160);\">（Nigel Coates）</span>可以称作是建筑叙事学的先驱，率先引导叙事在建筑与文学、电影之间的跨学科探索实践，研究如何利用建筑语言进行事件的描述和表达。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497048377254.jpg\" title=\"1602497048377254.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012115649_调整大小.jpg\" style=\"letter-spacing: 0.544px;\" /><br /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">虽然有专门研究建筑叙事学的学者，但是不同的建筑师也会根据自身的理论，在建筑叙事学的基础上进行不同方向和层面的探讨，我将其简单分为三种：</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: 16px;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1.再现</strong></span><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(160, 160, 160);\">（还原故事情节）</span>。即利用空间或者构造等某种建筑语言，再现某段历史情节，文学或电影故事等。<br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497062310730.jpg\" title=\"1602497062310730.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012115703_调整大小.jpg\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: 16px;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.重构</strong></span><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(160, 160, 160);\">（重组叙事结构）</span>。着重于对叙事结构和脚本而非故事内容进行分析，解构传统的空间叙事模式而将其重组，以获得新的建筑体验。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497074744210.jpg\" title=\"1602497074744210.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012115727_调整大小.jpg\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: 16px;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">3.介入</strong></span><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(160, 160, 160);\">（改变故事结果）</span>。通过观察社会矛盾，利用空间介入某种社会现象，从而达到组织和改善社会活动的目的。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang \n     <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong !important;\">丹尼尔·里伯斯金</strong>是一位大器晚成的建筑师。而柏林犹太人纪念馆则是他创业生涯浓墨重彩的一笔。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">从整体造型来看，建筑呈多重折线状，不规则的造型和尖锐的棱角使得更容易在人的心理上勾起沉重的情绪起伏。灵感来源于3000年前犹太人的大卫王朝的标志<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: 16px;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">大卫之星</strong></span>，只不过在这里，六角形的大卫之星被击碎，从而呈现出这样扭曲的造型。</p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; justify;\">轴线的终点并没有任何出口，等待着游客的是伸手不见五指的<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">死亡之塔</strong>，高耸的空间一篇漆黑，唯有顶部的一道缝隙艰难地透下一道光线，这并非是代表希望的光线，反而加深了底层的黑暗。<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">一种死亡的孤独感和沉重感扑面而来。</strong></span><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.流亡之轴</strong>。这条轴线通往室外的<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">霍夫曼公园</strong>，又是流亡者的花园，由倾斜的<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">49根混凝土方柱</strong>组成。倾斜的用意，是在于颠覆稳定的正交空间，令人感到头晕目眩，丧失方向感，不知何去何从。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">3.延续之轴</strong>。唯一能逃离地下一层走到其他展厅的，是延续之轴。在这条轴线上有一部长长的直跑楼梯直通三层，隐喻着犹太民族的延续。而<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">肆意穿刺的混凝土横梁</strong>架空在楼梯之上，分裂着这个高耸的空间，象征这条民族延续之路必定是<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">充满荆棘与坎坷</strong>的道路。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">叙事的意义不仅在于故事本身，也在于叙事结构的组织。有时通过将故事结构和叙事结构两者分离，重组再叠加，会给观者带来不同的故事体验。依然拿<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">诺兰</strong>的电影<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">《记忆碎片》</strong>为例，我们可以整理出这样两条结构：</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497335256238.jpg\" title=\"1602497335256238.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012120356_调整大小.jpg\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">上面一条为电影的时间顺序，而下面一条为故事本身的顺序。导演对两条结构线进行打散和重组，<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这意味着时间失去了结构整个故事的能力</strong>。前半个小时未必就是故事的伏笔，而后半小时也不一定是故事的结局。</p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497344223077.gif\" title=\"1602497344223077.gif\" alt=\"640 (11).gif\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">如果用建筑学的眼光来看，我们可以把电影的时间顺序想象成空间容器，而故事则为发生在空间中的一个个事件。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497355970215.jpg\" title=\"1602497355970215.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012120418_调整大小.jpg\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">因此我们可以发现，空间与空间中所发生的事件，并非一定是一一对应的，而这带来的体验，也必定是充满着随机性和偶然性的空间体验。<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">伯纳德·屈米便是这类思想的先驱。</strong></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在屈米的<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">《曼哈顿手稿》</strong>中，他把建筑分裂成三个系统：<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">空间系统，事件系统和运动系统</strong>，而分裂的意义，便在于以各种不同方式进行叠加，带来一种<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">蒙太奇</strong>的效果。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497364867167.jpg\" title=\"1602497364867167.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012120444.jpg\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这意味着，建筑不再被作者自身所定义，而是被其中所发生的运动和事件所定义。<br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">打个比方，圆形的空间，可以是神庙空间，也可以是福柯所说的监视与被监视的监狱空间。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497435747159.jpg\" title=\"1602497435747159.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012120502_调整大小.jpg\" style=\"letter-spacing: 0.544px;\" /><br /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">巴黎的街头，可以是休憩娱乐的公共空间，同样也可以是革命时期筑起战壕的斗争空间。空间是一个变化的容器。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497449499688.jpg\" title=\"1602497449499688.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012120514_调整大小.jpg\" style=\"letter-spacing: 0.544px;\" /><br /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这是<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">罗兰·巴特所</strong>谓的<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“作者的死亡”</strong>在建筑学中的反映。基于此伯纳德·屈米设计出了他的重要作品——<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">巴黎拉维莱特公园</strong>。在这个公园中，屈米抽离出点，线，面三层系统并相互叠加，以尝试获得非传统的空间体验。</p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497470804391.jpg\" title=\"1602497470804391.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012120553_调整大小.jpg\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497478373076.jpg\" title=\"1602497478373076.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012120608_调整大小.jpg\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: justify;\">1.点系统</span></strong><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: justify;\">。开放空间中的建筑本应是整体的样貌，这是传统的或者说是现代主义的结构，而屈米将其爆破，炸成一个一个碎片，散布在基址上一个120mx120m的方格网中，伫立于方格网内约40个交汇点上。他将其称之为 Folie (疯狂屋)。</span><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497485607086.gif\" title=\"1602497485607086.gif\" alt=\"640 (12).gif\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这与诺兰将一个完整的线性故事打碎重组有异曲同工之处。散布的疯狂屋又被瓦解成<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">27个更小的，边长为3.6米的立方体</strong>。</p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497492562862.gif\" title=\"1602497492562862.gif\" alt=\"640 (13).gif\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">去某些立方体，暴露出框架结构；</strong><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; !important;\">屈米设计了一套别致的道路系统以将各个片段串联在一起</strong>。除了两条平行于马路和河流的正交高架以外，大部分的公园道路都是没有逻辑的。</p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; \n  </section> \n  <section style=\"margin: 0px 0px 16px -12px; padding: 0px 10px 0px 20px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; display: inline-block; vertical-align: bottom; width: auto; min-width: 10%; flex: 0 0 auto; height: auto; align-self: flex-end; border-style: dashed; border-width: 0px 0px 1px; border-radius: 0px; border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62); z-index: 0;\"> \n   <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n    <section style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: justify; letter-spacing: 2px;\"> \n     <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">介入：西雅图图书馆</strong></p> \n    </section> \n   </section> \n  </section> \n </section> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">除了上述两种方式，叙事的意义还在于通过对现实描述而引发对现状的批判性反思。这要求讲述者具有宽广的眼界以洞悉全局，犀利的眼光以穿透表象。<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">雷姆·库哈斯</strong><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(160, 160, 160);\">（Rem Koolhaas）</span>虽然不是科班出身，但记者的早年生涯却赋予了他一般建筑师所不具备的<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">整体性</strong>和<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">结构性</strong>的社会眼光。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497647264094.jpg\" title=\"1602497647264094.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012120808_调整大小.jpg\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在库哈斯的眼里，建筑自身所能发挥的效应是有限的，但是建筑可以具有包容性，<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">与其创造出一种无欲无求的清教徒式的建筑，还不如利用社会，权力和资本</strong><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(160, 160, 160);\">（他认为这正是形成大都市的重要动力）</span><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">的力量接力打力，满足人们的欲求。</strong>因此他对大都市的多样性始终抱着一种好奇的实验性的目光。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: !important;\">他十分擅长处理复杂的多功能建筑，并从人和功能最基本的诉求出发，重新定义功能的实现方式。他所创立的<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">OMA</strong>出来过许多一流的建筑师，从倡导<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“Yes is more”</strong>的<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">BIG</strong>；</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; width: 338.5px;\"> \n  <section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: center;\"> \n   <section style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; vertical-align: middle; display: inline-block; line-height: 0;\"></section> \n  </section> \n </section> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">都或多或少地继承了库哈斯对功能与欲求两者关系的批判性思考。而<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">西雅图图书馆</strong>，可以说是库哈斯思想的代表作品之一。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497782394929.jpg\" title=\"1602497782394929.jpg\" alt=\"微信截图_20201012120919_调整大小.jpg\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: justify;\">什么是<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">图书馆</strong>？有以下三点需要论证：</span><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">① 以往的图书馆以藏书为目的，而在信息时代，电子书籍与纸媒共存，<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">因此图书馆便不再是关于“书本”的建筑，而是关于“阅读”的建筑。</strong></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497794984746.gif\" title=\"1602497794984746.gif\" alt=\"640 (19).gif\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">② 知识既然脱离了纸张，那就意味着有关“阅读”的图书馆<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">既要提供纸媒阅读的空间，也要提供电子阅览的空间。</strong></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">\n <img src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497802163059.gif\" title=\"1602497802163059.gif\" alt=\"640 (20).gif\" />\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">③ 媒介既然产生了变化，那么阅读的方式也不应再像过去的方式一样规规矩矩地被桌椅纸笔束缚，而更多是具备一种<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">休闲与灵活甚至是社交的气质，以应对不同和多变的阅读方式。</strong></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n</section> min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">基于以上三点，库哈斯尝试塑造出一种全新的阅读空间。他整理出五个巨大的功能体块，从下到上分别是<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">地下停车场，商店，会议区，藏书库，以及办公区。</strong></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p src=\"http://www.archcollege.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/1602497818644966.gif\" title=\"1602497818644966.gif\" alt=\"640 (22).gif\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">儿童活动区，出纳大厅，多功能大厅和开放阅览大厅。</strong></p>\n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" !important;\">公共空间与功能体块即分隔又上下交错，保证了公共空间不会因藏书规模的扩张而被挤压同时又具有良好的可达性。垂直的交通核和五颜六色的扶梯联系各功能上下。</p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, !important;\">两种功能之间也并非完全隔离，如公共空间中也存在书架，只不过书架的高度设计的极低，尽力去减少对空间多样性使用的干预，你可以在这里阅读传统书籍，也可以利用免费提供的400台电脑进行网上阅读且全部免费，当你读累了，这又是一个社交和休闲的空间。因此，阅读，这一简单功能经由库哈斯对社会发展的认知而被重新定义了。<br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; !important;\" /></p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: break-word !important;\">书库的设计同样别出心裁，因为坚持认为在现如今，<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">跨学科的学习和应用愈发重要</strong>，因此整个书库将不同科目的书籍放在了一起，并按书号的顺序，从“000”排到“999”，沿着螺旋状的坡道形成一条连续的书带，人们可以任意的在书库的各楼层间穿梭，大大节约了读者借阅的时间。</p> \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: !important;\">西雅图图书馆即是一座小城市，同时也是大城市的一部分。开放的公共空间吸引了当地的许多市民和流浪汉，在这个从资本积累转向信息积累的时代，这无疑从各方面实现了<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“全民图书馆”</strong>的含义。<br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; \n</section> \n<section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">任何叙事都存在三个角色：<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">讲故事的人，故事和听故事的人。</strong>建筑师作为叙事者，无论采用何种方式和主义进行叙事，都必须要保证建筑师本人对故事应当有着充分和全面的认知。而这其实已经是跳脱到专业知识以外的范畴，要求的也并不是建筑专业知识有多么独到，而是你对事件和现象的认知有多么深入。</p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">说到底，建筑学在这里只是一种工具，建筑也只是一种文本。如果没人听地懂，故事再巧妙精彩又有什么用呢？</strong></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(239, 73, 45);\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">完</strong></span></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(160, 160, 160); font-size: 12px;\">1.本文节选和改编自作者自己的小文《从建筑叙事学看社会关系与空间形构》</span></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(160, 160, 160); font-size: 12px;\">2.参考文献：《_以色列犹太人大屠杀纪念馆》，《_建筑叙事空间初探——以巴黎拉·维莱特公园为例》，《<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">_解读巴黎拉维莱特公园——多元背景下新型公园探索的一次解构实践</strong>》，《_建筑叙事学的缘起》，《_莱姆·库哈斯的建筑创作理念研究》等，此外还包括知乎的一个高赞回答《什么是建筑的叙事性？怎样的建筑才具有叙事性？》，只不过作者账号已注销…</span></p> \n <p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(160, 160, 160); font-size: 12px;\">3.所有模型分析图和动图均作者自绘，除此之外的图片包括实景照片，分析图均来源网络，包括知乎，百度等，由于本期图片实在太多就不一一列举，有想知道来源的可以留言。</span></p> style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(160, 160, 160); font-size: 12px;\">4.另外感谢同门：圣诞节 提供的《盗梦空间》故事图表~</span></p>
